Things got messed up when I found out that Kuya Sean likes Mitzie. I mean, yeah, the girl is beautiful and smart. She's my ideal girl, to be honest. Mahinhin tapos magaling pang kumanta.

Nagkaroon ako ng interes sa kanya hindi dahil gusto ko sya para sa akin kung hindi dahil nagustuhan sya ni Kuya na ang alam ay puro aral lang. Noong sabihin ko tuloy sa kanya na lalaban kami ay kung ano-ano na agad ang paalala nya na akala mo ay kasintahan nya ang babae.

Nang nasa library kami ni Mitzie para mag-aral, dumating si Sol na nakabusangot. I have to keep my eyes away from her to refrain myself from staring. I was drained when we finished reviewing our notes. Ngunit isang tingin ko lang sa nakangiting si Sol, para na akong natunaw.

It made me confused and mad.

"Tinanong ko lang naman kung pwedeng sa ibang araw na lang ang pamimili at pagbabake mo dahil sigurado naman akong hindi iyan importante!"

I immediately regretted saying it when I saw how pain passed through her eyes. I tried explaining to her but my words were useless. Nagsisi ako dahil nasaktan ko sya. I ought to protect her but I hurt her.

Still, she makes it up to me. Sya pa rin ang gumawa ng paraan para magkaayos kami. Iniiwasan ko sya dahil hindi na maganda ang nararamdaman ko sa kanya. I don't want to name it but my feelings are uncontrollable.

Things got even messier when I found out that Mitzie is pregnant with Kuya's child. Hindi pa nakatulong na binubugbog ito ng sarili nyang ama. Nanumbalik sa akin ang panahong puro sugat si Sol at wala akong magawa dahil masyado pa akong bata.

Lagi akong nasa tabi ni Mitzie na unti-unti na pala akong nawawala kay Sol.

"Si Sol oh..." bulong ni Mitzie sa akin habang nasa jeep kami.

Bumilis agad ang tibok ng puso ko at sumulyap sa itinuro nya. Nakita kong nagpapaulan si Sol kasama si Harvin. Gusto kong bumaba para pigilan ito ngunit malaki ang ngiti sa labi nya na parang masaya sya... doon ko rin napagtanto na may hawak itong kahon na naglalaman ng cheesecake na sa pagmamadali ay nailaglag ko kanina sa sahig ng classroom.

"Mukha ka nang bruha!" narinig kong malakas na sigaw ng lalaki na parang walang ibang nakatingin sa kanila. "Kumalat na ang mascara mo!"

"Ayos lang yan, maganda pa rin ako!"

I was hurt with what I saw. Solene always wants to run in the rain because she never experienced it as a child. Nakita ko kung paanong alalayan ni Harvin si Solene hanggang sa lumampas na ang jeep na sinasakyan namin sa kanila.

That same day, I admitted I fell in love with her.

Nang malaman kong nilalagnat sya, ginawa ko ang dating gawi namin. I went to her house and took care of her... only for her words to stab me. She doesn't want me anymore. She's so strong to give up on us.

"Do what you want, Duke. Hindi na kita haharangan."

Her words hit like a fucking train. Gusto kong sabihin sa kanya na may karapatan syang harangan ako dahil kaya nya akong kontrolin. I want to tell her my feelings.

And I did. It was the best decision I've ever made in my entire life. We show our love for each other in our own ways. We were happy and contented. Those were one of best moments I will treasure for the rest of my life.

Hindi mababayaran ang takot at pangamba ko nang hindi sya nagpakita. Lagi akong nakatanaw sa bahay nila dahil alam kong naroon lang silang dalawa ni Tita Yella. Nang pumasok sya sa school para magtake ng battery exam, saka lang ako nakahinga nang maluwag.

"Nandito lang ako... lagi para sayo..." I told her.

Pero laging mali. Laging may balakid. My heart got broken when she failed the battery exam. I wanted so bad to comfort and hug her... but I didn't. Instead, I ran after Mitzie to calm her down. Nasa isip ko noon, mas kaya ni Sol dahil hindi naman mahina ang loob nya.

And I regret it so much. I hurt her again. Just when I was about to make it up to her, everything got tangled up.

"Duke, bro! Magpapakamatay ata si Mitzie!" ani Calix sa akin sa telepono.

Naging mabilis ang pagkilos ko. Ni hindi ko na nasabihan ang mga kakilala o kaibigan dahil sa pagmamadali. Marami nang tao ngunit walang pumipigil sa babae. Kita kong may malaking foam sa baba ng building para kung sakaling matuloy ang pagtalon ay ligtas pa rin ito. Ngunit hindi ko maiwasang mag-alala sa dinadala nitong bata. Kuya Sean is messing things up!

"Stop acting like you care for me, Duke! Kay Solene ka lang may pakealam!"

"I care for you, Mitzie. Alam mo yan," pang-aalo ko.

"But you love her more!" Sigaw nya. "Hindi naman kita gusto pero dahil kang nandyan para saken, hindi ko maiwasang mahalin ka! Dahil lagi mo akong pinipili kumpara sa kanya, nahuhulog ako sayo!"

Pinigilan ko ang sarili na magpakita ng kung anong reaksyon. She's with my brother!

"Do you love her?!" tukoy nya kay Sol.

I want to tell the truth but I'm afraid it would trigger her more.

"N-no, Mitz, I-I don't love her..."

I swear to God, I didn't mean it. I love Solene more than my own life! But I have to deny it. I have to calm and tame her. Pamangkin ko ang nasa loob ng tyan nya at hindi ko kakayanin kung may masamang mangyayari sa bata.

I said words I could never take back. She's insecure of Sol... my love... but she's in the verge of death and I can't afford seeing her in that state when I know I can do something.

My world crumbled down when I found out that Sol is listening with whatever bullshit I was saying. My trembling hands reached hers but she shoved it away. 

"Girlfriend mo ako pero ilang beses mo nang ipinaramdam sa akin na mas mahal mo si Mitzie..."

It crashed me. I love Sol so much but I started discarding her.

"Sol... hindi..." umiling ako nang paulit-ulit. Walang ibang lumalabas sa bibig ko dahil sa halo-halong emosyon. Nangingibabaw ang takot dahil alam kong masisira kami pagkatapos nito... and I will bleed.

I wanted to tell her that she's the best for me, the most beautiful and all but words failed me. Habang pinapanood ko syang umiiyak ay tumutulo rin ang luha sa mga mata ko, walang pakealam sa mga estudyanteng nanonood.

"Ang galing mo!" sigaw nya sa akin. "Para iligtas sya, kailangan mong lunurin ako!"

Para akong sinasakal habang sinasabi nya iyon. No, baby, I didn't mean that. I love you so much...

I saw her gulped. "Maghiwalay na tayo."

And that's how I ruined my life. Nawala sya matapos ang gabing iyon. I spent my nights on bars to drink liquors because I always see her face in my room. She left me and I fucking deserve it!

Sa tapat ng bahay nila ako madalas... umaasang bigla syang magbubukas ng pinto. Wala na akong pakealalam kahit hindi sya maging akin... basta nakikita ko sya. Ayos lang na hindi ko sya maabot basta alam kong nasa paligid lang sya.

Pero hindi. She vanished.

"Anak, nakausap ko ang dean nyo, kaunti na lang ay mawawala ka na sa candidates ng mga makaka-receive ng latin honor."

That seems to push me back to my track. A year later, I found myself apologizing to Troy because he was seriously mad at me for hurting Sol. I was mad at myself too but now, my inspiration to do better will be her.

"Buti at natauhan ka. Sayang ang pag-aaral mo at ikaw lang ang minamatang Magna Cum Laude ng batch natin," ani Mitzie sa akin.

Naging ayos din kami. Mahabang usapan iyon kasama si Kuya pero hindi ko na masyadong pinagtuunan ng pansin.

"Ayokong pagbalik ni Sol ay maaabutan nya ako nang ganoon. Hindi sya matutuwa..."

She dropped her eyes on her phone. I know that guilt and regret are eating her system. Naging matalik din silang magkaibigan pero dahil sa nangyari ay nawala ang babae.

I graduated with latin honors. My family and friends were happy for me. Umuwi rin si Papa para sa graduation ko at naayos ang gulo sa pamilya namin tungkol sa pambababae nito. It was like a mini reunion.

Pero kahit anong gawin ko, hinahanap ng mga mata ko ang isang babae na may kulay tsokolateng buhok, maputing balat, masungit na mukha at mainit na ngiti... but again, she isn't here.

I earned money to renovate their house. I did it secretly because I don't want people to think about it. I hired Ate Ivy to maintain the cleanliness of the area.

It was hard. Hindi pa ako malaki kumita pero ayun ang unang-una kong ipinagawa. This place will always have a special place in our hearts.

Five years after her disappearance, Mitzie rushed towards me.

"May page pala si Sol! She's a baker now! Wala pang sariling shop pero maraming customers!"

Agad kong tiningnan ang hawak nyang cellphone at nag-init ang dalawang sulok ng mga mata ko nang makita sya sa larawan.

I caressed her cheeks as if those were real.

"My Sol..." I whispered to myself. She's smiling widely at a customer while holding a medium-sized cake.

I became her constant follower since that day. Sa dami siguro ng followers nya ay hindi nya na napansin ang pangalan ko. I always visit her page to see updates of her. Hindi sya nagpopost ng picture nya. Talagang mga niluluto nya lang ang ginagawa nya.

Call me a creep but I watched her from afar. Hindi ako makalapit dahil bukod sa naduduwag pa ako, wala pa akong napapatunayan. Oo, engineer na ako ngunit hindi pa ako nabibigyan ng magandang break.

"I'm Bethany... you're Engr. Laurence, right?"

Inabot ko ang palad nya at bahagyang napangiwi sa itinawag nya sa akin.

"Call me Duke."

She grinned. "Okay, Laurence."

Bethany somehow reminds me of Sol. Mahilig ito sa chicken curry at magaling din magbake. She got my interest at first but it was shortlived. Napagtanto ko rin agad na wala akong ibang gusto kung hindi si Solene.

"I'll go to Amsterdam and you'll come with me!" bungad nya sa akin isang umaga sa opisina ko.

Binasa ko ang pang-ibabang labi at umiling. "Busy ako, Beth. Marami pa akong hindi naaayos na blueprints."

It was partly true. Ngunit ang pinaka pinagkakaabalahan ko ay ang nalalapit na pagharap kay Sol. I was promoted as head engineer at sa akin inassign ang malaking tulay at shortcut ng Las Islas hanggang La Union. It was a huge project and many engineers envied me.

Nagbukas ng shop si Sol at nagbabalak akong pumunta sa grand opening nito.

"Ganon?" malungkot na tanong ni Bethany.

I nodded. I have a lot on my plates right now.

But when I saw Sol's update about joining an international convention on Amsterdam, I immediately texted Bethany.

Me:
I will go with you.

Bethany:
Yay! Ang lakas ko talaga sayo!

"I had a childhood friend who loves eating cheesecakes so I started learning baking." Solene said in an interview.

I know it was me. I'm her only childhood friend who loves cheesecakes. The familiar warmth embraced me as I remember the young version of her, learning how to bake because I said I love cheesecakes.

Kitang-kita ko ang pagguhit ng gulat sa maganda nyang mukha nang ipakilala ako ni Bethany. Kahit dinadaga ang dibdib ko, pinanatili ko ang seryosong mukha.

Our meetings in Amsterdam aren't the best because she pushes me away every damn time! I get it but I'm still human! My heart didn't take it lightly when I heard her talking to a guy named Atreus and her voice sounded so nice. Ilang mura ang pinigilan ko dahil sa mga napagtanto.

Maaaring wala itong kasintahan ngayon ngunit sigurado akong maraming nag-aabang sa kanya.

Still, I pursue her. I courted her because this is the only chance I got. I love her that even if I see her being comfortable with Atreus, I endured it.

"Don't even think of flirting with Sol," paalala ko kina Tim, James at Angelo nang utusan ko silang bumili ng merienda namin.

They exchanged a knowing look and grinned. "Si Angelo ang may gusto kay Miss Sol, Engineer!"

Takot na umiling si Angelo sa akin lalo at nasalubong ang tingin ko. Kung pwede lang ay ako na ang magpupunta roon para makita na rin si Sol. Ang kaso lang ay mag-iikot ang mga architect sa site at kailangan ko silang samahan.

Bethany found out that I'm courting Solene and she isn't happy with it. Nagulat pa ako noong minsang pumunta ito sa unit ko nang lasing.

"Beth, umuwi ka na sa inyo. Ihahatid na kita."

Umiling sya. "No! You break my heart, Laurence! Para ka ring si Atreus!"

Inalalayan ko sya patayo mula sa couch ko ngunit kinuha nya ang braso ko. Dahil sa gulat ay napahiga ako sa katawan nya. Nang hinalikan nya ako ay mabilis akong umalis sa ibabaw nya. Galit na galit akong tumingin sa kanya ngunit nakapikit na sya at parang natutulog.

Hindi lang iisang beses nangyari iyon. May isang beses na kahit hindi sya lasing ay hinahalikan nya ako. My reaction is consistent. I always push her away. Para sa akin ay kaibigan ko ang babae at wala dapat mamagitan sa amin. Isa pa, nililigawan ko si Sol at hindi magandang tingnan na ginaganito nya ako.

Sol❤:
si atreus na ang maghahatid sa akin, don't bother

Nasa labas na ako ng shop nya nang itext nya iyon. I saw her being guided by Atreus towards his car. Bumigat ang loob ko dahil ito ang pinili nyang maghahatid sa kanya kahit na ako ang nauna.

Nagulat ako nang malamang sa Laguna rin pala ang delivery nito at kina Kuya Sean pa! That night, I fell harder. Kahit na nalaman ko ang mga pinagdaanan nya sa interview nya sa Amsterdam, nasasaktan pa rin ako lalo at narinig kong nabastos sya.

"I don't need you here... umuwi ka na..."

Her words linger but I know she's deeply affected by Atreus' accident. Those days were painful. Nilimitahan nyang makipagkita sa akin ngunit dahil hindi ko kayang wala akong ginagawa para sa kanya, pagkatapos sa trabaho ay magluluto ako para ibigay sa guard. Kapag hindi masyadong busy, tumutulong ako sa shop nya dahil hindi na sya nakakapasok.

"Naku, Engineer, 'yung nililigawan mo, may ibang inaalagaan."

My forehead creased at the terms used. "Kaibigan nya iyon, Tim. Natural lang na nandoon sya habang nagpapagaling ito."

"Hirap magmahal nang ganyan!"

I ignored his remarks. Hindi ko na rin masyadong makausap si Sol kaya inasikaso ko ang pagfifile ng kaso laban sa nambastos sa kanya noon.

Sol❤:
I'm sorry to say this to you, Duke, but you should stop pursuing me. Pasensya na kung hindi ko sa personal nasabi ito sayo pero sa paggising ni Atreus, sasagutin ko na s'ya.

That ended me. Para akong bumalik sa dating gawi na puro inom ang ginagawa para makalimot. I love her so much but she doesn't want me anymore. She loves someone else now.

Gusto kong maging makasarili at ipagsiksikan ang sarili ko sa kanya ngunit hindi ko kayang pagkaitan sya ng kasayahan na matagal nya na dapat nararanasan. Masakit dahil alam kong tuluyan na akong nawalan ng pag-asa para maipakita sa kanya ang pagmamahal ko.

I went to Greece. Kinumbinsi ko ang sarili na dahil iyon sa offer na pagrerenovate sa pinakamalaking tulay pero alam kong para sa kanya kaya ako umalis. Her predator is wandering around this place and I have to track him down.

Isa pa, ayokong makita sya na may kasamang... hindi ako.

For a year, I busied myself with work and her case. Pumunta pa si Bethany sa Greece para iparinig sa akin ang testimonies ng ibang biktima. I tried focusing on her lalo at nagbibigay sya ng motibo ngunit hindi ko talaga kaya. Pakiramdam ko ay may niloloko ako.

"Come on, Laurence... we're both single." She uttered in a very sexy voice.

Bethany is beautiful. Her features are soft but with her red and plump lips, you will know that she isn't a typical soft girl.

I want to try but I didn't. My thoughts were clouded by Sol and my love for her. Pakiramdam ko ay hindi ko na kayang magmahal.

"Gago ka! You're cheating on her?! With her friend?! Sol doesn't deserve an asshat like you!"

Nakaupo na sa semento si Atreus dahil sa lakas ng suntok ko. Nagdilim ang paningin ko nang makitang may kalandian ito sa mall. At buntis pa talaga! Kaya siguro pansin na pansin ko ang lungkot sa mata nya nung nasa club kami... hinayaan nya pang may gagong humalik sa kanya.

Nagdadalawang isip pa ako noong una kung sasabihin ko iyon kay Sol pero sa dulo ay sinabi ko rin. And her revelations shocked me.

Me, being the smitten piece of a crap, I tried again. I pursued her again. It's like a never-ending chase but I know I can never love the same way again. She's my ball of sunshine.

I did my best. I showed her my purest intentions. Hindi matatawaran ang saya ko nang malamang nagpunta sya sa Greece para sa akin.

I want to kiss her that night... but I don't have the right yet.

"Mahal ko po si Duke."

Para akong nabuhay ulit nang marinig iyon. She said it so softly as if the words were fragile glasses. Nang humarap sya sa akin at nakita ko ang mapula nyang pisngi ay may kung anong kumurot sa loob ko.

She's so beautiful and radiant. Her warmth is something you will get addicted to. She's as serene as the sunrise... the one you'll look forward to for the rest of your life. The beauty of her eyes was like sunset... they will make you feel like there's an untold promise that tomorrow will get better.

She doesn't realize how beautiful she is... like the sun.

Ngayon ay nasa harap kaming dalawa ng puntod ni Tita Yella. The sexual harassment case was closed and Matthew will spend the next years of his life in a prison cell. Atreus and Jelay welcomed their baby girl. Si Bethany naman ay nagpaplano sa pagtatayo ng sarili nyang law firm ngunit nagkaroon ng gap ang pagkakaibigan namin.

But it's okay.

Hindi ko nagustuhan ang ginawa nya pero ngayong nasa akin na si Sol, parang kaya kong magpatawad.

When I found out that Tita Yella committed suicide, I cried with Sol. We hugged each other that night and prayed for her mother's soul.

"Ang gusto nyo lang po ay ligawan ko si Sol pero... I want more than that, Tita." I said while holding my baby's hand. "I'm sorry for inflicting pain to your precious daughter. I'm undeserving... but years passed and I'm still so in love with her. Nothing has changed." I'm really hopeless.

I sighed, a bit teary. "She's still the one I prayed for. It hurt me that she gave herself to me but I failed to keep her."

Naramdaman kong pinisil nya ang kamay ko at tumalon ang puso ko roon.

"I won't do it this time, Tita. I will love her better."

Tumingin ako sa kanya at halos matulala na naman ako sa ganda nya.

"I will marry you."

With tears in her eyes, she nodded slowly and planted a kiss on my lips. I supported her waist and lean closer to her.

I have chased the sun... my sun.

        
Chapter 44 - Note

            Thank you for sticking with me 'til the end!

This is a story of love, dreams, family and forgiveness. I know that all of you already know this but, really, no man is an island. No matter how tough a person might be, at the end of the day, everyone needs a helping hand. Also, your life might not go according to your plan but that doesn't mean you've failed. You're meant for something greater and more profound.

Always choose happiness without hurting anyone in the process.

I hope that you learn something from our Solene and Duke Laurence. I wanted to impart to you that love isn't too dreamy but I also want you to appreciate their emotional, behavioral and mental development.

Lastly, this story has a lot of typographical and grammatical errors... at wala pa akong plano kung kailan ko 'to pwedeng i-edit.

I'm the type of person who writes impulsively kaya may ibang parts sa story na 'to na baka hindi ko o niyo nagustuhan. But still, I managed to finish writing it so I'm really glad. This is my first finished novel and this will always be a special thing to me. Marami rin akong natutunan habang isinusulat 'to. Hindi perfect ang plot, dialogues at conflicts... pero that's how we grow.

Again, thank you for riding with Duke and Sol!

I love you, my inks!

PS: See you on Taming the Waves (College Series#2)!♥
